

*"Be cheerful also, and seek not external help nor the tranquility which others give. A man then must stand erect, not be kept erect by others."*

— **Marcus Aurelius**

*"Be cheerful also, and seek not external help nor the tranquility which others give. A man then must stand erect, not be kept erect by others."*

— **Marcus Aurelius**
